Increasing temperature could lead to more randomness, which encourages more diverse or creative outputs.\n\nYou are essentially increasing the weights of the other possible tokens. In terms of application, you might want to use a lower temperature value for tasks like fact-based QA to encourage more factual and concise responses. For poem generation or other creative tasks, it might be beneficial to increase the temperature value."
